<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kovàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковать.html>кова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выковать.html>вы́ковать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подковать.html>подкова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forge
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выковать.html>вы́ковать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výkovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>

***ковер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковёр</a> (2557)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/sv:Jooseppi_Julius_Mikkola" class="extiw" title="w:sv:Jooseppi Julius Mikkola">Jooseppi Julius Mikkola</a>, quoted by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Max_Vasmer" class="extiw" title="w:Max Vasmer">Vasmer</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Karl_Brugmann" class="extiw" title="w:Karl Brugmann">Karl Brugmann</a><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>, asserts that it is from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">kǫgurr</i><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>. A Turkic origin has also been theorised. Compare Romanian <i class="Latn mention" lang="ro">covor</i> (lt;Russian), Slovak and Czech <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">koberec</i>, Polish <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kobierzec</i>, archaic Bulgarian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">губер</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">guber</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковёр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kovjór</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковра́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковры́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковер.html>ковро́в</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковровый.html>ковро́вый</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коврик.html>ко́врик</a></b>)

***коверкать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:коверкать.html>кове́ркать</a> (26577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:коверкать.html>кове́ркать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kovérkatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:исковеркать.html>искове́ркать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mispronounce words and sounds
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1969</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%91%D1%83%D0%BB%D0%B3%D0%B0%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2,_%D0%9C%D0%B8%D1%85%D0%B0%D0%B8%D0%BB_%D0%90%D1%84%D0%B0%D0%BD%D0%B0%D1%81%D1%8C%D0%B5%D0%B2%D0%B8%D1%87" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Булгаков, Михаил Афанасьевич">Булгаков</a>,  chapter 1, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9C%D0%B0%D1%81%D1%82%D0%B5%D1%80_%D0%B8_%D0%9C%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B3%D0%B0%D1%80%D0%B8%D1%82%D0%B0" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Мастер и Маргарита"><a href = vnd.unilang:мастер.html>Ма́стер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:маргарит.html>Маргари́та</a></a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:извинить.html>Извини́те</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пожалуйста.html>пожа́луйста</a>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:заговорить.html>заговори́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подошедший.html>подоше́дший</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иностранный.html>иностра́нным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:акцент.html>акце́нтом</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:коверкать.html>кове́ркая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́в</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Izvinite menja, požalujsta, — zagovoril podošedšij s inostrannym akcentom, no ne <b>koverkaja</b> slov</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Excuse me," began the man who had approached them. He had a foreign accent, but did not <b>mispronounce</b> any words</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> familiar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break, to destroy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to recite one's opponent's speech with mistakes; to distort another's speech</li></ol>

***ковчег.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковчег.html>ковче́г</a> (23448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ковьчегъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kovĭčegŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Mongol" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Mongol">Middle Mongolian</a></span> <i class="Mong mention" lang="xng">ᠬᠠᠤᠷᠴᠠᠭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xng-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">qaurčag</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> presumably through a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mongolian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Mongolian language">Mongolian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="mn">хуурцаг</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="mn-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">huurtsag</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковчег.html>ковче́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kovčég</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковчег.html>ковче́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковчег.html>ковче́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковчег.html>ковче́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ark
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Ноев <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ковчег.html>ковче́г</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nojev <b>kovčég</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Noah's ark</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ковчег.html>ковче́г</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:завет.html>заве́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>kovčég</b> zavéta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Ark of the Covenant</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>shrine</li></ol>

***ковш.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковш.html>ковш</a> (13095)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ковшь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kovšĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">káušas</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ladle, dipper, big spoon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">káuti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hew, chop out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*káuˀtei</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kowh₂-</i>, from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kewh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковш.html>ковш</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kovš</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковш.html>ковша́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковш.html>ковши́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковш.html>ковше́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>scoop, dipper, ladle</li>
<li>bucket <i>(of an excavator)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ковы.html>ко́вы</a> (28453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковать.html>кова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковы.html>ко́вы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kóvy</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковы.html>ко́в</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> intrigues, machinations</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковылять.html>ковыля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kovyljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ковыльну́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">доковыля́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заковылять.html>заковыля́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">приковыля́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проковыля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hobble, to dodder, to toddle, to stump
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:уйти.html>уйти́</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ковылять.html>ковыля́я</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ujtí, <b>kovyljája</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hobble off/away</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ковырять.html>ковыря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kovyrjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to peck <i>(at)</i>, to pick <i>(at)</i>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tinker</li>
<li>to dig</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ря́<span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ю<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щий<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>Возвра́тное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:настоящий.html>настоя́щего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ковыр-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-я-ющ</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b>.
</p>

***когда.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> (45)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*koda</i>, from which the following words also were derived: Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">къгда</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kŭgda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Bulgarian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">кога</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">koga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Polish <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kiedy</i>, Serbo-Croatian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">када</i> / <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">kada</i>, Czech <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">kdy</i>, Polish <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">gdy</i>, Lower Sorbian <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">gdy</i>. Originally the word was probably *koda; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">kada</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">when</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">kad</i>, Old Indic and Hindi <i>कदा</i> (kəda), Avestan <i>kadā</i>. From *koda came *kъdа, possibly under the influence of *kъdе, kъtо. On the other hand, one may perceive in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kogdá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> the old instrumental singular *godō of the word <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">god</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (the old meaning of which was “time, period”) with the interrogative particle ко-, making a genitive singular form *kogo goda (which time?). Thus the -гда ending may have derived from the genitive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">god</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">period of time</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kogdá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>when
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приехать.html>прие́хали</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Kogdá</b> vy prijéxali?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">When did you arrive?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kogdá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>when
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne znáju, <b>kogdá</b> éto býlo.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don’t know <b>when</b> it was.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Both the subordinate clause with the conjunction <b><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></b> and the main clause can have either an imperfective or a perfective verb. However, the whole context of the respective sentences could be different due to the difference of the aspects.</li>
<li>Chiefly in colloquial language, the conjunction <i><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a></i> can be moved to any position in the dependent clause including the final one; this typically occurs in short introductory clauses that recall or specify being in the middle of things of a situation.</li></ul>

<p><b>ког<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да́</a></b>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когорта.html>кого́рта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kogórta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когорта.html>кого́рты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когорта.html>кого́рты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когорта.html>кого́рт</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cohort</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гора.html>го́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та</a></b>

Зализняка).

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:кодак.html>ко́дак</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***кодировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кодировать.html>коди́ровать</a> (26759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kodieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кода.html>код</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kod</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодировать.html>коди́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kodírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодировать.html>коди́ровать</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закодировать.html>закоди́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to code, to encode, to encrypt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодирующий.html>коди́рующее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устройство.html>устро́йство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kodírujuščeje ustrójstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">coder; (en)coding device</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give hypnotic/suggestive treatment <i>(for alcoholism, etc)</i></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:кодировка.html>кодиро́вка</a> (24002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодировать.html>коди́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kodírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодировка.html>кодиро́вка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kodiróvka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодировка.html>кодиро́вки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодировка.html>кодиро́вки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодировка.html>кодиро́вок</a></b>)
</p>
